route-policy IT_IN
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0) and not next-hop in (10.159.255.5, 10.159.255.6, 10.159.255.17, 10.159.255.18) then
    drop
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any comm_99_p1_permit) and (destination in pfx_IT_IN_p1_permit)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any comm_99_p1_permit) then
    drop
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any comm_98_p1_permit) and (destination in pfx_IT_IN_2_p1_permit)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any comm_98_p1_permit) then
    drop
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any comm_97_p1_permit) and (destination in pfx_IT_IN_3_p1_permit)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any comm_97_p1_permit) then
    drop
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any comm_96_p1_permit) and (destination in pfx_IT_IN_Gy_p1_permit)) then
    pass
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any comm_95_p1_permit) and (destination in pfx_IT_IN_probe_p1_permit)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any comm_95_p1_permit) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy

  if destination in FIB-DROP-SHT-PREFIXES or destination in FIB-DROP-SNW-PREFIXES then
    pass
  else
    # Route-policy to prevent selected IPCORE and IPRAN prefixes into FIB due to CSCvr41333
    if destination in FIB-DROP-PREFIXES then
      drop
    else
      pass
    endif
  endif
end-policy

    set extcommunity rt CD_S1U_DEF_RT
  elseif destination in CD_S1U_Digi_Core then
    set extcommunity rt CD_S1U_KPG_HUB_RT
  elseif destination in CD_S1U_ZTE_RAN_Sarawak then
    set extcommunity rt CD_S1U_BORNEO_SPOKE_RT
  elseif destination in CD_S1U_ZTE_RAN_Sabah then
    set extcommunity rt CD_S1U_BORNEO_SPOKE_RT
  elseif destination in Digi_MC_S1U_Digi_RAN_Sabah then
    set extcommunity rt CD_S1U_BORNEO_SPOKE_RT additive
  elseif destination in Digi_MC_S1U_Digi_RAN_Eastern then
    set extcommunity rt CD_S1U_BORNEO_SPOKE_RT
  elseif destination in Digi_MC_S1U_Digi_RAN_Northern then
    set extcommunity rt CD_S1U_BORNEO_SPOKE_RT
  elseif destination in Digi_MC_S1U_Digi_RAN_Southern then
    set extcommunity rt CD_S1U_BORNEO_SPOKE_RT
  elseif destination in Digi_MC_S1U_Digi_RAN_Sarawak then
    set extcommunity rt CD_S1U_BORNEO_SPOKE_RT additive
  elseif destination in Digi_MC_S1U_Digi_RAN_Central then
    set extcommunity rt CD_S1U_BORNEO_SPOKE_RT additive
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy CD_S1U-Import-RT
  if (destination in CD_S1U_Celcom_Core) then
    pass
  elseif (destination in CD_S1U_Borneo_Celcom_Core) then
    pass
  elseif (destination in Digi_MC_S1_Celcom_RAN_Sabah) and (extcommunity rt matches-any Digi_MC_S1) then
    pass
  elseif (destination in Digi_MC_S1_Celcom_RAN_Sarawak) and (extcommunity rt matches-any Digi_MC_S1) then
    pass
  elseif (destination in Digi_MC_S1_Celcom_RAN_Central) and (extcommunity rt matches-any Digi_MC_S1) then
    pass
  elseif (destination in Umobile_Core_MC_S1U_Pfx01) and (extcommunity rt matches-any (65535:65602)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any Digi_MC_S1) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
